Amazon Pay Feature Reference - boundary test fixture.
This document enumerates Amazon Pay product features, generated for upload-size boundary testing.

Amazon Pay Feature: One-Click Checkout. Allows a returning customer to complete a purchase in a single click using their saved Amazon Pay address and payment method. The feature is part of the Amazon Pay platform and integrates with the customer wallet, merchant settlement pipeline, fraud and risk engines, and the reconciliation and reporting subsystem. It honors RBI guidelines on tokenization, two-factor authentication and storage of customer instruments, and exposes both REST and SDK surfaces for merchant integration. Operationally the feature emits structured events for downstream analytics, billing and customer-support tooling.

Amazon Pay Feature: Buy Now Pay Later. Customers split eligible Amazon Pay purchases into interest-free EMIs at checkout, with eligibility decided in real time. The feature is part of the Amazon Pay platform and integrates with the customer wallet, merchant settlement pipeline, fraud and risk engines, and the reconciliation and reporting subsystem. It honors RBI guidelines on tokenization, two-factor authentication and storage of customer instruments, and exposes both REST and SDK surfaces for merchant integration. Operationally the feature emits structured events for downstream analytics, billing and customer-support tooling.

Amazon Pay Feature: UPI Payments. Amazon Pay UPI lets users link any UPI-enabled bank account and pay merchants, scan QR codes, and send money to contacts. The feature is part of the Amazon Pay platform and integrates with the customer wallet, merchant settlement pipeline, fraud and risk engines, and the reconciliation and reporting subsystem. It honors RBI guidelines on tokenization, two-factor authentication and storage of customer instruments, and exposes both REST and SDK surfaces for merchant integration. Operationally the feature emits structured events for downstream analytics, billing and customer-support tooling.

Amazon Pay Feature: Recurring Payments. Subscription mandates over UPI AutoPay and cards-on-file allow merchants to debit customers on a fixed schedule. The feature is part of the Amazon Pay platform and integrates with the customer wallet, merchant settlement pipeline, fraud and risk engines, and the reconciliation and reporting subsystem. It honors RBI guidelines on tokenization, two-factor authentication and storage of customer instruments, and exposes both REST and SDK surfaces for merchant integration. Operationally the feature emits structured events for downstream analytics, billing and customer-support tooling.

Amazon Pay Feature: Amazon Pay Wallet. Closed-loop wallet for instant settlements on Amazon and partner merchants, with KYC-driven top-up limits. The feature is part of the Amazon Pay platform and integrates with the customer wallet, merchant settlement pipeline, fraud and risk engines, and the reconciliation and reporting subsystem. It honors RBI guidelines on tokenization, two-factor authentication and storage of customer instruments, and exposes both REST and SDK surfaces for merchant integration. Operationally the feature emits structured events for downstream analytics, billing and customer-support tooling.

Amazon Pay Feature: Send Money to Contacts. Peer-to-peer transfers to phone-number or VPA addresses, with instant credit on the recipient bank account. The feature is part of the Amazon Pay platform and integrates with the customer wallet, merchant settlement pipeline, fraud and risk engines, and the reconciliation and reporting subsystem. It honors RBI guidelines on tokenization, two-factor authentication and storage of customer instruments, and exposes both REST and SDK surfaces for merchant integration. Operationally the feature emits structured events for downstream analytics, billing and customer-support tooling.

Amazon Pay Feature: Bill Payments. Pay electricity, water, gas, broadband and postpaid bills with reminders and auto-pay opt-in across 100+ billers. The feature is part of the Amazon Pay platform and integrates with the customer wallet, merchant settlement pipeline, fraud and risk engines, and the reconciliation and reporting subsystem. It honors RBI guidelines on tokenization, two-factor authentication and storage of customer instruments, and exposes both REST and SDK surfaces for merchant integration. Operationally the feature emits structured events for downstream analytics, billing and customer-support tooling.

It honors RBI guidelines on tokenization, two-factor authentication and storage of customer instruments, and exposes both REST and SDK surfaces for merchant integration. It honors RBI guidelines on tokenization, two-factor authentication and storage of customer instruments, and exposes both REST and SDK surfaces for merchant integration. It honors RBI guidelines on tokenization, two-factor authentication and storage of customer instruments, and exposes both REST and SDK surfaces for merchant integration. Operationally the feature emits structured events for downstream analytics, billing and customer-support tooling.
